Only music was able to lift her out again -- showing her that her goal needn't be to play lofty concert halls, but instead to bring the wonder of the instrument to as many people as possible.

TEDTalks is a daily video podcast of the best talks and performances from the TED Conference, where the world's leading thinkers and doers give the talk of their lives in 18 minutes (or less). Look for talks on Technology, Entertainment and Design -- plus science, business, global issues, the arts and much more.

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function() {

            $(".signin").click(function(e) {          
				e.preventDefault();
                $("div#signin_menu").toggle();
				$(".signin").toggleClass("menu-open");
            });
            $(".signin").mouseover(function(e) {          
				e.preventDefault();
                $("div#signin_menu").show();
				$(".signin").addClass("menu-open");
            });
            $(".signin").mouseout(function(e) {
                return false;
            });  
			
			$("div#signin_menu").mouseup(function() {
				return false
			});
			$(document).mouseup(function(e) {
				if($(e.target).parent("a.signin").length==0) {
					$(".signin").removeClass("menu-open");
					$("div#signin_menu").hide();
				}
			});			
			
        });
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   /* For the home page */
$(function(){
   $('.plusBtn, .plusBtn1').each(function(){
        
		var img = $(this).closest('li').find('img:first');
        //alert(img);
        //document.write(img);
        var courseID    = '0';
		$(this).click(function(){
		   if( $(this).hasClass('courseQueueAdder') ){
                courseID    = $(this).data('course');
                //alert(courseID);
            }else{
                //alert("no course")
            }
            //return false;
          
			
            /* Handle the click event */
            if( logged == '0' ){
               showPrompt("Please log in to add to your Queue.", "Confirmation");   
               return false; 
            }
            var video_id    = $(this).attr('rel');
            var prevCount   = parseInt($("#queue_counter").text());
            $.ajax({
                url     : 'http://www.courseworld.org/home/add_to_queue',
                data    : {'video_id':video_id, "course_id":courseID},
                type    : 'POST',
                success : function(resp){
                    //alert(resp);
                    if(resp == '3'){
                        //alert("Please log in to add to your Queue.");
                        showPrompt("Please log in to add to your Queue.", "Confirmation");
                        return false;
                    }else if(resp == '2'){
                        if( courseID != "0"){
                            //alert("This course is already added to your queue !");
                            showPrompt("This course is already added to your queue!", "Confirmation");
                        }else{
                            //alert("This video is already added to your queue !");
                            showPrompt("This video is already added to your queue!", "Confirmation");
                        }
                        
                        return false;
                    }else if(resp == '1'){
                        flyToElement($(img), $('#basket'));
                        $("#queue_counter").text(prevCount+1);
                        /*if( courseID != "0"){
                            alert("Video added to your queue");
                        }else{
                            alert("Course added to your queue");
                        }*/
                    }else{
                        return false;
                    }
                },
                error   : function(resp){
                    //alert("Some error occured, Try again. ");
                    showPrompt("Some error occured, Try again.", "Confirmation");   
                }
            });
            /* Handle the click event */
			return false;
		});

	}); 
});
/* For the home page */

/* For the video details page */
$(function(){
   $("#queueAdder").live('click', function(){
        if( logged == '0' ){
           showPrompt("Please log in to add to your Queue.", "Confirmation");   
           return false; 
        }
        var img = $(this).find('img:first');
        /* Handle the click event */
        var video_id    = $(this).attr('rel');
        var prevCount   = parseInt($("#queue_counter").text());
        $.ajax({
            url     : 'http://www.courseworld.org/home/add_to_queue',
            data    : {'video_id':video_id},
            type    : 'POST',
            success : function(resp){
                //alert(resp);
                if(resp == '3'){
                    //alert("Please log in to add to your Queue.");
                    showPrompt("Please log in to add to your Queue.", "Confirmation");   
                    return false;
                }else if(resp == '2'){
                    //alert("This video is already added to your queue !");
                    showPrompt("This video is already added to your queue!", "Confirmation"); 
                    return false;
                }else if(resp == '1'){
                    flyToElement($(img), $('#basket'));
                    $("#queue_counter").text(prevCount+1);
                    //alert("Video added to queue");
                    showPrompt("Video successfully added to your queue.", "Confirmation"); 
                }else{
                    return false;
                }
            },
            error   : function(resp){
                //alert("Some error occured, Try again. ");
                showPrompt("Some error occured, Try again.", "Confirmation");    
            }
        });
        /* Handle the click event */
   }); 
});

/* For the video details page */
function flyToElement(flyer, flyingTo, callBack /*callback is optional*/) {
	var $func = $(this);

	var divider = 3;

	var flyerClone = $(flyer).clone();
	$(flyerClone).css({
		position: 'absolute',
		top: $(flyer).offset().top + "px",
		left: $(flyer).offset().left + "px",
		opacity: 1,
		'z-index': 1000
	});
	$('body').append($(flyerClone));

	var gotoX = $(flyingTo).offset().left + ($(flyingTo).width() / 2) - ($(flyer).width()/divider)/2;
	var gotoY = $(flyingTo).offset().top + ($(flyingTo).height() / 2) - ($(flyer).height()/divider)/2;

	$(flyerClone).animate({
		opacity: 0.4,
		left: gotoX,
		top: gotoY,
		width: $(flyer).width()/divider,
		height: $(flyer).height()/divider
	}, 700,
		function () {
			$(flyingTo).fadeOut('fast', function () {
				$(flyingTo).fadeIn('fast', function () {
					$(flyerClone).fadeOut('fast', function () {
						$(flyerClone).remove();
						if( callBack != null ) {
							callBack.apply($func);
						}
					});
				});
			});
		});
}

function showPrompt(txt, title){
    $.prompt.close;
    $.prompt(txt, {
    	title: title,
    	buttons: { "Ok, got it!": true }
    });
}

function queueInit(){
    $('.plusBtn, .plusBtn1').each(function(){
        
		var img = $(this).closest('li').find('img:first');
        //alert(img);
        //document.write(img);
        var courseID    = '0';
		$(this).click(function(){
		   if( $(this).hasClass('courseQueueAdder') ){
                courseID    = $(this).data('course');
                //alert(courseID);
            }else{

            }
            //return false;
          
			
            /* Handle the click event */
            if( logged == '0' ){
               showPrompt("Please log in to add to your Queue.", "Confirmation");   
               return false; 
            }
            var video_id    = $(this).attr('rel');
            var prevCount   = parseInt($("#queue_counter").text());
            $.ajax({
                url     : 'http://www.courseworld.org/home/add_to_queue',
                data    : {'video_id':video_id, "course_id":courseID},
                type    : 'POST',
                success : function(resp){
                    //alert(resp);
                    if(resp == '3'){
                        //alert("Please log in to add to your Queue.");
                        showPrompt("Please log in to add to your Queue.", "Confirmation");
                        return false;
                    }else if(resp == '2'){
                        if( courseID != "0"){
                            //alert("This course is already added to your queue !");
                            showPrompt("This course is already added to your queue!", "Confirmation");
                        }else{
                            //alert("This video is already added to your queue !");
                            showPrompt("This video is already added to your queue!", "Confirmation");
                        }
                        
                        return false;
                    }else if(resp == '1'){
                        flyToElement($(img), $('#basket'));
                        $("#queue_counter").text(prevCount+1);
                        /*if( courseID != "0"){
                            alert("Video added to your queue");
                        }else{
                            alert("Course added to your queue");
                        }*/
                    }else{
                        return false;
                    }
                },
                error   : function(resp){
                    //alert("Some error occured, Try again. ");
                    showPrompt("Some error occured, Try again.", "Confirmation");   
                }
            });
            /* Handle the click event */
			return false;
		});

	});
}

     <div style="float:left;padding-top:10px;">
      <p id="video_desc" style="text-align: justify;overflow: hidden;height: 86px;width:720px!important">
       In her quest to become a world-famous violinist, Ji-Hae Park fell into a severe depression. Only music was able to lift her out again -- showing her that her goal needn't be to play lofty concert halls, but instead to bring the wonder of the instrument to as many people as possible.

TEDTalks is a daily video podcast of the best talks and performances from the TED Conference, where the world's leading thinkers and doers give the talk of their lives in 18 minutes (or less). Look for talks on Technology, Entertainment and Design -- plus science, business, global issues, the arts and much more.
Find closed captions and translated subtitles in many languages at http://www.ted.com/translate

Follow TED news on Twitter: http://www.twitter.com/tednews
Like TED on Facebook: https://www.facebook.com/TED

Subscribe to our channel: http://www.youtube.com/user/TEDtalksDirector

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(function(){
    $("#mailchimpFrmFooter").validationEngine({
        promptPosition          : 'topLeft',
        'custom_error_messages' : {
            '#subscribe_email'    : {
                'required'  : {
                    'message'   : ' *Please enter your email'
                },
                'custom'     : {
                    'message'   : '*Please enter a valid email'
                }
            }
        },
        onValidationComplete    : function(form, status){
            $("#error").fadeOut();
            if(status){
                $.ajax({
                    type    : 'POST',
                    data    : $("#mailchimpFrmFooter").serializeArray(),
                    url     : base_url+'get_involved/subscribe',
                    beforeSend : function(){
                        $("#subscribe_email_footer").addClass('searchLoading');
                    },
                    success : function(resp){
                        $("#subscribe_email_footer").removeClass('searchLoading');
                        if(resp == '1'){
                            $("#subscribe_email_footer").val("");
                            $.prompt('You are already in our mailing list!', {title:"You're Done!"});
                        }else if(resp == 2){
                            $.prompt('You are now subscribed to our mailing list!', {title:"You're Done!"});
                            $("#subscribe_email_footer").val("");
                        }else{
                            $.prompt("Oops, that didn't work. Please try again.", {title:"Error!"});
                            $("#subscribe_email_footer").val("");
                        }
                    },
                    error   : function(resp){
                        $.prompt("Oops, that didn't work. Please try again.", {title:"Error!"});
                        $("#subscribe_email_footer").val("");
                    }
                });
            }

        }
    });
})
  </script>
